`+k8s:prerelease-lifecycle-gen:replacement=<group>,<version>,<kind>` tags on types\\n- Auto-generates APILifecycleDeprecated(), APILifecycleRemoved(), and APILifecycleReplacement() methods on affected types\\n- Auto-generated methods produce zz_generated.prerelease-lifecycle.go files across the codebase\\n\\n## Enforcement Workflow\\n\\n1. API types define lifecycle information through build tags in their type definitions\\n2.
